[02-Mar-22 02:36 AM] ApexChat#8127
**DrMambo**:	There is a â€œworkforce reserve poolâ€ of a certain size on each planet. This means a percentage of workers of each workforce tier will not be distributed automatically but is held back. Workers from the reserve pool can be recruited instantly during the week by building a new production building that requires them. However, each player can only instantly recruit a small percentage of the pool for themselves every week. (Note: If there are more players requiring workers of a certian tier than there are workers, these workers will be added to the reserve pool as well.)

[06-Apr-24 10:05 PM] ApexChat#8127
